2651f5c4-d9e1-4b06-92be-e9e7313f87c4

asio.sys

Description

Confirmed vulnerable driver from Microsoft Block List

  • UUID: 2651f5c4-d9e1-4b06-92be-e9e7313f87c4
  • Created: 2023-01-09
  • Author: Nasreddine Bencherchali, Michael Haag
  • Acknowledgement: |

DownloadBlock

This download link contains the vulnerable driver!

Commands

sc.exe create asio.sys binPath=C:\windows\temp\asio.sys type=kernel &amp;&amp; sc.exe start asio.sys
Use Case Privileges Operating System
Elevate privileges kernel Windows 10
